Acki Nacki Announcements 08.10.2024 19:00:58
In reply to this message
üåü Acki Nacki just cut its blockchain minimum Node requirements in half.

Acki Nacki ‚Äî fastest blockchain possible ‚Äî announced the refactoring of its node software to allow the network to run on even lower specs üåü

Now, minimum requirements for Block Keeper Nodes that anyone can buy have gone down to 8c/16t CPU, 64 GB RAM, 1 TB NVMe Storage, and 1 Gbit synchronous unmetered Internet connection.

Subsequently, the cost of running the Node is cut by more than tree times, to a monthly total lowest cost of around $75 to $150 for Block Keeper consensus node.

That is 4 times less than Solana while being 20 times more performant within these specs.

üëπ Acki Nacki wants everyone to be able to join the network: To participate, mine, and prevent large concentrations of network ownership, because true decentralization happens when many people own, govern with, and HODL the network tokens.

The new specs are available in these docs:

Install rust
curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh


Install node-helper
cargo install --git https://github.com/ackinacki/ackinacki.git node-helper


Generate BLS/ed25519 keys par
mkdir -p ~/.secret
node-helper bls --path ~/.secret/block_keeper_bls.json
node-helper gen-keys --path ~/.secret/block_keeper_ed25519.json


Look at the created key files in a way convenient for you and say the public part, for example like this
jq -r .public ~/.secret/block_keeper_bls.json 
jq -r .public ~/.secret/block_keeper_ed25519.json


#bls #ed25519
